***pip.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pip.html>pip</a> (12521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pip.html>pip</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">disease of poultry, also of people</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from post-classical <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pipita</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pītuīta</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slime, head cold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_9">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pip.html>pip</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:pip.html>Pip</a></a> (any of various respiratory diseases in <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a>, especially infectious coryza).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">humorous or colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of humans, a disease (particularly the common cold or the flu), <a href = vnd.unilang:malaise.html>malaise</a> or depression.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_3">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pips.html>pips</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pip.html>pip</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>krijgen</a></span></li></ul>
<hr />

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pip.html>pip</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> / <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">pirate</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">pirate</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pīrāta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πειρατής</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peiratḗs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πεῖρα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peîra</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trial, attempt, plot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pispot.html>pispot</a></i>. <p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pistache.html>pistache</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pistache.html>pistaches</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pistache.html>pistachetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>The pistachio tree (<i>Pistacia <a href = vnd.unilang:vera.html>vera</a></i>)</li>
<li>Its greenish, edible nut-like fruit; also sugared etc. as candy</li>
<li>A sweet resembling the above candy</li>
<li>The fruit's taste, also as a flavor, notably of ice cream

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pistool.html>pistool</a> (776)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">píšťala</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whistle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*piščalь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*piskati, *piščati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to squeak, whistle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*pīṣk-</i>.

***plaats.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a> (452)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">plāetse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">place</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plaatsen.html>plaatsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaatsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">place</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">position</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plek.html>plek</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A settlement; a town, city, village, <a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>hamlet</a> or the like.</li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">place</span>, a <span class="Latn" lang="en">location</span> in a text.</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">Space</span>, especially free space (e.g. volume, area or storage space on a medium).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:extensie.html>extensie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:neemt.html>neemt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:beslag.html>beslag</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This extension <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> up a lot of <b>space</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">square</span>, a <span class="Latn" lang="en">plaza</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">paved open space of any size in a town or near a building</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plein.html>plein</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">farm</span>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boerderij.html>boerderij</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">boerenplaats</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plagerij.html>plagerij</a> (114020)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plagen.html>plagen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to plague; to tease</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erij</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Or alternatively, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plager.html>plager</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">plaguer; <a href = vnd.unilang:teaser.html>teaser</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ij</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also the usage notes at <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erij</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plagiaat.html>plagiaat</a> (28544)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">plagiat</i>.

***plakken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plakken.html>plakken</a> (7735)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">placken</i>, further etymology unknown. Cognates are found only in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">placken</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plakken.html>plakken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stick</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to glue, to paste</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to paste (insert an item previously <a href = vnd.unilang:saved.html>saved</a> to memory)</li></ol>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">beplakken</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">opplakken</span></li></ul>

***planeet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:planeet.html>planeet</a> (1461)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">planete</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">planete</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">planēta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πλανήτης</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">planḗtēs</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wanderer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***planten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:planten.html>planten</a> (3386)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:planten.html>planten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">planton</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">planter</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">plantō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:planten.html>planten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to plant, place a seed or plant in suitably fertile substrate in order that it may live and grow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to plant an inanimated object in the soil or a hard surface, e.g. a banner</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to plant an idea etc.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">planter</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">plantgoed</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">plantstok</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">aanplanten</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beplanten.html>beplanten</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">neerplanten</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">verplanten</span></li></ul>
